               <p>女儿上中学后,<span class="label-words" data-wid="871">个子</span>长得特别快,现在都快一米六了,<span class="label-words" data-wid="754">差不多</span>跟她妈妈一样高了。</p>

              <div class="text-center field-subject ans-hide">
               <p>在<span class="label-words" data-wid="953">加油站</span>或者离<span class="label-words" data-wid="953">加油站</span>很近的地方<span class="label-words" data-wid="773">抽烟</span>、打手机，是很<span class="label-words" data-wid="1243">危险</span>的。<span class="label-words" data-wid="1316">因此</span>，<span class="label-words" data-wid="833">法律</span><span class="label-words" data-wid="899">规定</span><span class="label-words" data-wid="953">加油站</span><span class="label-words" data-wid="981">禁止</span><span class="label-words" data-wid="773">抽烟</span>和<span class="label-words" data-wid="1168">使用</span>手机。</p>
              </div> 
              <div class="text-center field-question">
               <p>★ <span class="label-words" data-wid="953">加油站</span>不<span class="label-words" data-wid="1350">允许</span>打手机。</p>
              </div>

              <div class="text-center field-subject ans-hide">
               <p>我刚才<span class="label-words" data-wid="1200">算</span>了一下，每个月的房<span class="label-words" data-wid="1411">租</span>、<span class="label-words" data-wid="967">交通</span>费、电话费、上网费，再加上水费、电费<span class="label-words" data-wid="809">等</span>，<span class="label-words" data-wid="1383">至少</span><span class="label-words" data-wid="806">得</span>一千两百块。</p>
              </div> 
              <div class="text-center field-question">
               <p>★ 房<span class="label-words" data-wid="1411">租</span>每个月一千二。</p>

              <div class="field-subject ans-hide">
               <p>不是<span class="label-words" data-wid="1132">任何</span>事情都需要<span class="label-words" data-wid="977">解释</span>。有时候，太多的<span class="label-words" data-wid="977">解释</span><span class="label-words" data-wid="748">不仅</span>不会得到别人的<span class="label-words" data-wid="1033">理解</span>，<span class="label-words" data-wid="1264">相反</span>，还可能会<span class="label-words" data-wid="1357">增加</span><span class="label-words" data-wid="1254">误会</span>。已经<span class="label-words" data-wid="831">发生</span>的事情是<span class="label-words" data-wid="859">改变</span>不了的，<span class="label-words" data-wid="1380">只要</span>自己做得<span class="label-words" data-wid="1366">正确</span>，<span class="label-words" data-wid="1417">最后</span><span class="label-words" data-wid="1406">自然</span>会得到别人的<span class="label-words" data-wid="1371">支持</span><span class="label-words" data-wid="1336">与</span><span class="label-words" data-wid="1278">信任</span>。</p>
              </div>

                 </div> 
                </div>
               </div>
              </div> 
              <div class="field-subject ans-hide">
               <p>“天外有天，人外有人”的意思是，当我们认为自己在哪<span class="label-words" data-wid="842">方面</span>很<span class="label-words" data-wid="1325">优秀</span>时，不要<span class="label-words" data-wid="968">骄傲</span>。因为这个世界很大，很可能有人在这<span class="label-words" data-wid="842">方面</span>比我们更<span class="label-words" data-wid="1038">厉害</span>。你在这<span class="label-words" data-wid="842">方面</span>是第一，并不<span class="label-words" data-wid="792">代表</span>你在每个<span class="label-words" data-wid="842">方面</span>都是第一。<span class="label-words" data-wid="1049">另外</span>，你现在是第一，也不<span class="label-words" data-wid="792">代表</span>你<span class="label-words" data-wid="1322">永远</span>都是第一。</p>
              </div>
             </div> 
             <div class="field-body">

               <p>新闻<span class="label-words" data-wid="724">报道</span>就是对最近<span class="label-words" data-wid="831">发生</span>的事情的<span class="label-words" data-wid="724">报道</span>。它有三个<span class="label-words" data-wid="1220">特点</span>:<span class="label-words" data-wid="1178">首先</span>，要新鲜，必须是最新<span class="label-words" data-wid="1270">消息</span>；<span class="label-words" data-wid="1101">其次</span>，要<span class="label-words" data-wid="1403">准确</span>，必须是<span class="label-words" data-wid="1163">实际</span><span class="label-words" data-wid="1115">情况</span>；<span class="label-words" data-wid="1417">最后</span>；必须是热点，必须是大家关心的问题。只有这样，新闻才会有<span class="label-words" data-wid="1256">吸引</span>力。</p>

              <div class="field-subject">
               <p>说话是一门<span class="label-words" data-wid="1314">艺术</span>，<span class="label-words" data-wid="1339">语言</span>是人们<span class="label-words" data-wid="738">表达</span><span class="label-words" data-wid="1000">看法</span>、<span class="label-words" data-wid="966">交流</span><span class="label-words" data-wid="867">感情</span>的<span class="label-words" data-wid="873">工具</span>。看一个人怎么说话，<span class="label-words" data-wid="1242">往往</span>可以比较<span class="label-words" data-wid="1403">准确</span>地<span class="label-words" data-wid="1087">判断</span>出他是一个什么样的人。有的人心里怎么想，<span class="label-words" data-wid="1415">嘴</span>上就怎么说，<span class="label-words" data-wid="942">即使</span>是对别人的<span class="label-words" data-wid="1123">缺点</span>，他也会<span class="label-words" data-wid="1373">直接</span>说出来，这样的人给人<span class="label-words" data-wid="865">感觉</span>很<span class="label-words" data-wid="770">诚实</span>；有的人虽然也看到别人的<span class="label-words" data-wid="1123">缺点</span>，但<span class="label-words" data-wid="1125">却</span>不会<span class="label-words" data-wid="1373">直接</span><span class="label-words" data-wid="1381">指</span>出来，<span class="label-words" data-wid="829">而</span>是<span class="label-words" data-wid="1229">通过</span>别的<span class="label-words" data-wid="841">方法</span>来<span class="label-words" data-wid="1223">提醒</span>，让你认识到自己的<span class="label-words" data-wid="1123">缺点</span>，这样的人会让人觉得更<span class="label-words" data-wid="1331">友好</span>。</p>

             </div> 
             <div class="field-footer">
              <div class="field-answer ans-hide">
               <label>Đáp án đúng:</label>
               <p>最好不要直接拒绝别人的邀请。</p>
              </div> 
              <div class="field-user-answer">
               <label>您的答案:</label>
              </div> 
              <div class="field-reviews">
               <label>Giải thích:</label>
               <p>根据词意，谓语动词是“拒绝”，“直接”表示“拒绝”的方式，作状语放在“拒绝”之前，“不要”是否定副词，放在谓语动词“拒绝”之前，“最好”表示意愿，也是放在“拒绝”之前，副词、方式状语和能愿词的顺序就是“最好不要直接”，“邀请”是“拒绝”的宾语，“别人的”是“邀请”的定语，所以正确答案就是：最好不要直接拒绝别人的邀请。</p>
              </div> 
              <div class="field-counter">
               Câu hỏi này được trả lời 8186 lần, tỉ lệ đúng là 34%
              </div>
             </div>
            </div>
           </div>

               <div class="field-option-wrap inline">
                <div class="field-option" data-index="1">
                 <p><span class="label-words" data-wid="764">吵</span><span class="label-words" data-wid="1285">醒</span>了</p>

             <div class="field-footer">
              <div class="field-answer ans-hide">
               <label>Đáp án đúng:</label>
               <p>他被外面的敲门声吵醒了。</p>
              </div> 
              <div class="field-user-answer">
               <label>您的答案:</label>
              </div> 
              <div class="field-reviews">
               <label>Giải thích:</label>
               <p>这是一个被字句，先找出“吵醒”这个动作的发出者和受事者，分别是“外面的敲门声”和“他”，我们知道被字句中动作的发出者作句子的宾语，受事者作句子的主语，所以正确答案就是：他被外面的敲门声吵醒了。</p>
              </div> 
              <div class="field-counter">
               Câu hỏi này được trả lời 7985 lần, tỉ lệ đúng là 65%
              </div>

               <label>Đáp án đúng:</label>
               <p>这是一个关于顾客和售货员的笑话。</p>
              </div> 
              <div class="field-user-answer">
               <label>您的答案:</label>
              </div> 
              <div class="field-reviews">
               <label>Giải thích:</label>
               <p>量词“个”后面应该是名词“笑话”，而“关于”后面又是一个具体的内容，所以组成“一个关于顾客和售货员的笑话”，“这是”明显在句子开头，所以正确答案是：这是一个关于顾客和售货员的笑话。</p>
              </div>

              <div class="field-answer ans-hide">
               <label>Đáp án đúng:</label>
               <p>职业和专业并没有太大关系。</p>
              </div> 
              <div class="field-user-answer">
               <label>您的答案:</label>
              </div> 
              <div class="field-reviews">
               <label>Giải thích:</label>
               <p>我们知道固定搭配“并没有/不”，所以这里“并”后面是“没有”，而“关系”一般是两个或者两个以上的事物之间的联系，所以根据意思我们知道正确答案是：职业和专业并没有太大关系。</p>

               <p>那位出租车师傅对这儿非常熟悉。</p>

              </div> 
              <div class="field-reviews">
               <label>Giải thích:</label>
               <p>“位”是量词，这里是修饰“师傅”，组成“这位出租车师傅”，“熟悉”作谓语，“对这儿”介宾短语一般要放在谓语前面，所以得出答案：那位出租车师傅对这儿非常熟悉。</p>

               <label>您的答案:</label>
              </div> 
              <div class="field-reviews">
               <label>Giải thích:</label>
               <p>“提供”做谓语，“饮料”是宾语，根据这个我们得出：火车上提供免费的饮料，“吗”是句末语气词，表示疑问的语气，所以正确答案是：火车上提供免费的饮料吗？</p>
              </div>

$('#exercise-list').exerciseTest({"submit":"/vi/4/4/submit?lid=70","submitParams":{"recent_index":0}});

        var paperDate = new Date(), stopOffsetDate, timeLeft = 6000, timeTotal = 6000;
        paperDate.setSeconds(paperDate.getSeconds() + 6000);
        $('#paper-countdown').on('click', '.btn[data-op]', function () {
            var op = $(this).data('op');
            if(op === 'start' && stopOffsetDate){
                paperDate = new Date();
                paperDate.setHours(paperDate.getHours() + stopOffsetDate.hours);
                paperDate.setMinutes(paperDate.getMinutes() + stopOffsetDate.minutes);
                paperDate.setSeconds(paperDate.getSeconds() + stopOffsetDate.seconds);
                $('#paper-countdown').countdown('setFinalDate', paperDate);
            }
            $('#paper-countdown').countdown(op).find('.btn[data-op]').toggleClass('hide');
            $('#exercise-list').exerciseTest('resetTime');
        }).countdown(paperDate, function (event) {
            timeLeft = event.offset.hours * 60 * 60 + event.offset.minutes * 60 + event.offset.seconds;
            $('.cd-time', this).html(event.strftime('%H:%M:%S'));
        }).on('stoped.countdown', function (event) {
            stopOffsetDate = event.offset;
        });
        $('#exercise-list').on('slid.bs.carousel', function (e) {
            var $el = $(e.relatedTarget), index = $el.index();
            $('#exr-prev').prop('disabled', $el.prev().length === 0);
            if ($el.next().length > 0) {
                $('#exr-next').removeClass('hide');
                $('#exr-submit').addClass('hide');
            } else {
                $('#exr-next').addClass('hide');
                $('#exr-submit').removeClass('hide');
            }
            if (!$el.data('autoPlayed')) {
                $el.find('.circle-audio').autoPlay();
                $el.data('autoPlayed', 1);
            } else if (e.direction === 'left') {
                $el.prev().stopPlay();
            } else {
                $el.next().stopPlay();
            }
            $(this).exerciseTest('setSubmitParams', 'recent_index', index);
            activeAnswerSheetPanel(index);
        }).on('slide.bs.carousel', function (e) {
            $('.item.active .exercise-view', this).trigger('next.hsk.test');
        }).on('beforeSubmit', function (e) {
            e.submitParams.duration = timeTotal - timeLeft;
        });
        $('#exr-submit').on('click', function (e) {
            if(window.confirm('确定要提交试卷吗?')){
                $('.item.active > .exercise-view', '#exercise-list').trigger('next.hsk.test');
                $('#exercise-list').exerciseTest('submit', true).done(function (data) {
                    window.location.href = '/vi/4/4/report?pid=' + data.exam_id;
                });
            }
        });
        function activeAnswerSheetPanel(index) {
            var $collapse = $('li[data-slide-to=' + index + ']', '#answer-sheets').closest('.collapse');
            if (!$collapse.hasClass('in')) {
                $collapse.prev('.panel-heading').find('[data-toggle=collapse]').trigger('click');
            }
        }
        activeAnswerSheetPanel(0);
        window.setTimeout(function () {
            $('.item.active', '#exercise-list').data('autoPlayed', 1).find('.circle-audio').autoPlay();
        }, 1000);
    
jQuery('#emw-34fcb4d5').modal({"show":false});
jQuery('#emw-34fcb4d5').on('show.bs.modal', function(event){
    if(event.relatedTarget){
        var el = $(event.relatedTarget), url = el.attr('href') || el.data('url'), frm = $('iframe', this), 
        self = $(this), e = $.Event('beforeLoading.wm', {relatedTarget: el, url: url, loadingUrl : url});
        self.trigger(e);
        if(frm.data('_url') !== e.url){
            var title = el.data('title') || el.attr('title');
            title && $('.modal-title', this).html(title);
            frm.attr('src', e.loadingUrl).data('_url', e.url).parent().addClass('loading');
            self.trigger('afterLoading.wm', e.loadingUrl);
        }
    }
}).find('iframe').on('load', function() {
    $(this).height($(this.contentDocument).height()).parent().removeClass('loading');
});
});</script>  
 </body>
</html>
